 So let's know those 5 reasons which are probably behind the popularity of Taarak Mehta's Overseas Eyeglasses
 realistikatarak mehta kaa ulta chashma kii story line behad hi pyor or realistic si he
 This show connects people
 is sho main daily shope kii tarah saas bahu drame ko jagah nahin di gai he

 aaj ke daur main log drame kii bajaay acha or vaastavik lagane vaale contate kii taraf rukh kar rahe hai
 In such a situation, this show connects people well

 Almost every plot of theirs ends on some social message

 ye sho har jenereshan ko hit karata he

 Drinking organic tea once or twice a day can be beneficial but too much caffeine will increase your discomfort
 2
 Do not touch alcohol, taking alcohol during periods can increase the discomfort
 periods main alcohol lene se pet kaa nichalaa hissaa phool jaataa he
 3
 chocolate khaane se bhi bachenchocolate main caffeine hota he, jisaki vajah se cramping kii problem bad sakati he
 Caffeine causes the muscles to contract, which can increase the pain
 4
 Avoid eating red meat
 Eating red meat increases the pain during periods
 red meet main maujuud acids prostate glands ko bahut active kar dete hai
 Due to which the pain during periods increases
 5
 Make too much sour things during the distance period can be dangerous
 khaastaur par namakeen or achaar
 Actually, a lot of sodium is found in these things, due to which the pain increases
 prastaavit ahmedabad-mumbai bullate train project ke ek mahatvapurn stesan sabarmati ko khaas tareeke se dizin karne kaa faisla kiya gaya he
 The design of the Sabarmati Bullet Train Station will bear the full imprint of Mahatma Gandhi's Dandi March in 1930
 neshnal hai speed railway karporation limited (enechaesarsiel) ne is stesan kii dizin kii pariklpana kii pehali tasviren saamne rakhi hai
 a special design has been prepared showing the freedom movement of Mahatma Gandhi at the Sabarmati Bullet train station
 pariklpana ke mutabik jab is stesan ko upar se dekhenge to aapako charakhe kii tasviir spasht taur par najar aegi
 The expenditure of 250 crores used to be Mahatma Gandhi's ashram in Sabarmati present in Gujarat, from where he agitated the whole country for the independence of the country
 mahatma gandhi ko sabarmati kaa sant bhi kaha jaataa he
 According to MD Achal Khare of Bullet Train Project, it will cost about two hundred and fifty million rupees to build Sabarmati Bullet Train Station
 unhone bataaya ki stesan kshetra main 3 level kii parking kaa bandobast kiya jayega
 There will be parking of about 150 vehicles
 pehle level par kaaron ke liye parking hogi, duusare level par bason kii or tisare level par auto rickshaw kii parking kii vyavastha kii jaaegi
 According to Achal Khare, Sabarmati Bullet train station will also be given connectivity with the railway station and two metro stations

 gujarat, maharashtra or dadar nagar haveli main jila prashasan ko us jameen kii suchi bhej di gai he jisko adhigrahit kiya janaa he

 jaisalmayr se 120 kilometre dur or mata tanot mandir se 5 kilometre pehle mata ghantiyali kaa darbar he
 BSF soldiers are worshiped by Mata Bellayali and Mata Tanot
 1965 kii jang main mata kaa aisa chamatkaar dikhaa ki pakistani sena vahiin dher ho gai
 It is said that the Pak army fought each other as enemies, Pak soldiers entered the temple of Mata and got involved in a mutual dispute and Pak soldiers became blind in the third miracle
 kitna purana he mandirmandir ke mukhya pujari bhi biguef sipaahi hi hai
 His name is Pandit Sunil Kumar Awasthi
 avasthi kii maane to mandir 1200 varsh purana he
 Mata's miracle here is that during the 1965 war, the Pakistani Army, considering its own army as an Indian soldier, started firing on each other
 kuch pakistani sainik ghantiyali matamandir takapahunch gai thi
 When the temple was damaged, there was another miracle of the mother and due to mutual dispute, all the Pakistani soldiers died fighting and fighting among themselves
 avasthi ne bataaya ki ghantiyali tak pahunchi ek anya pakistani tukdi ne mata ghantiyaali kii murti kaa shringaar utaarne kii koshish kii to ve sabhi andhe ho gaye the
 These are 10 famous temples of Maa Durga, BSF worships Poojamata Bellayali and Mother Tanot worshiped by BSF soldiers
 1965 or 1971 kii jang main donon deviyon ke aashirwad se tathaa chamatkaar se pakistaniyon ko dhul chataane ke baad biguef ne dononmandiron kaa jimmaapane haathon main le liya
 In both temples, only the BSF soldier is a priest
 abhi yah jimmedaari biguef kii 135veen vahini ke paas he

 to dusri ore sarhad par lagaataar golabari bhi kiye ja rahaa he

 iske baad pakistan kii ore se loc par lagaataar sijafire kaa ulanghan kiya ja rahaa he
 It was fired 35 times in two days
 bataa den, pakistan kii ore se airstrike ke baad se lagaataar golabari kii ja rahi he
 Pakistan fired mortars on Thursday for the seventh day
 ek adhikari ne bataaya ki pakistan kii is karatuut se ek mahila kii maut ho gai or ek jawan ghayal ho gaya
 Retaliation is also being done on behalf of India
 raksha pravaktaa ne kaha ki pakistan kii sena ne lagaataar jammu-kashmir ke sunderbani, manakot, khaari karmaara, degavaar sectoron main baari golabari or choti hathiyaaron kii golabari kii he
 The fire started from 6 am on Thursday
 iske baad loc par ruuk-ruuk pakistan kii ore se golabari kii gai
 The Indian Army responded strongly and effectively
 saal 2018 main loc par pakistan sena sabase zyada sijafire kaa ulanghan kiya tha
 He had last fired around 2,936 times
 adhikari ne kaha ki pakistan donon deshon ke seemaa suraksha balon ke bich flag meeting ke dauraan sanyam baratane or samjhaute kaa paalan karne ke vaade ke baad bhi sijafire kar rahaa he
 In the current era, while many traditional crafts are struggling to save their existence, on the other hand, a small village called Ajrakhpur in Kutch, Gujarat is attracting domestic and international buyers with block-colored fabrics dyed with their natural bright colors
 is print ko ajrakh ke naam se janaa jaataa he, jise banane main kaaphi samay va parishram lagata he or yah ek lambii prakriya he
 More than a hundred families of the village are associated with this craft, after which the highest quality cloth is prepared, and then it is labeled the top company of fashion
 gujarat ke mukhyamantri rahete hue pradhanmantri narendra modi ne is gaanv kii kala ko badhaava dene kaa aashwaasan diya tha
 According to Sufiyan Ismail Khatri, who settled in Ajrakpur from Dhamdaka village after the devastating earthquake in Bhuj in 2001, this village is not very old, but his craft is more than 400 years old
 sufian ajrakh printer kii 9veen peedi se hai
 They have preserved the art of their ancestors till date, which their ancestors brought here from Sindh
 ek shilpkaar ko dizin sikhaate hue sufian ne kaha, "prakritik rangon ke madhyam se paaramparik ajrakh priting 16 charnon kii prakriya he
 It takes 14 to 21 days
 yah is baat par bhi nirbhar karata he ki isamen kitne rang honge or block print ke kitne staron kaa istemaal kiya jayega
 " kapadon ko daai karne se pehle unhen pani main puri raat bhigoya jaataa he, taaki unamem se atirikt starch nikal jaae
 They are then dried in the sun
 sookhne ke baad unhen mayobralam rang se ranga jaataa he, jiske baad phir se unhen dhoop main sookhne ke liye rakh diya jaataa he
 After the completion of this process, craftsmen choose wooden blocks with traditional designs and then glue them carefully onto the cloth with the help of glue
 ajrakh printig main kapade par block rakhane ke baad use dabaakar rakhana hota he
 Similarly, craftsmen choose blocks, color them and carefully place them on clothes and press them
 yah prakriya puri hone ke baad kapadon ko dhokar dhoop main sukhaya jaataa he
 All the colors used in clothes are made in a natural way
 ajrakh ko arabi bhashaa main indigo kaha jaataa he, jiskaa arth nil kaa paudha hota he
 This plant was visible everywhere in the area before the 1956 earthquake in Kutch
 lekin, kuch shilpakaaron kii maane to ajrakh shabd 'aaj rakh' se aayaa he
 You will see a large amount of iron sawdust around the Ajrakhpur workshop
 lohe ke chure main gud or besan milakar kaala rang banaaya jaataa he
 Another craftsman from the village, Ismail Anwar, said that it takes at least 15 days to make this color
 imali ke beej or fitkaree se laal rang banaaya jaataa he
 Turmeric is a yellow color and lime is used to make white
 anwar ne kaha, "paramparaagat rup se ajrakh printig keval prakritik rangon se hi kii jaati thi, lekin ab sasti kism kii maang ke chalate isamen kritrim rangon kaa bhi istemaal kiya jaataa he
 Pintering done with artificial colors takes less time
 " He said that it takes two days to prepare a saree with artificial pintering
 jab kabhi maal kii zyada maang hoti he, to isi kaa istemaal kiya jaataa he
 a fabric made of artificial colors costs 50 to 60 rupees per meter, but if the fabric is printed with a unique design, then the price can go up to 100 rupees per meter
 ajrakh kii kahani hameshaa se itani rangarang nahin thi
 There was also a bad time in the lives of these craftsmen, when all the craftsmen had to give up everything and move to another place and start living life again and put all the resources back
 sufian ne bataaya, 'aaj hamaare shilp kii bazaar main bahut maang he
 Designers like Tarun Tahiliani have worked with me
 diziners ke aamantran par mujhe alag-alag jagah jaakar apni kala dikhaane ke maukey mili
 Today, big designers of the world want to know about our art
 " Anwar said that many children come from the designer institute to learn their art
 duniyabar ke sabhi karigar unki pradarshnee dekhne aate hai
 He said that his work does not stop in any season, whether it is winter or summer
 unka yah kaam april maheene kii tej garmi main bhi chalata rahata he, kyonki kaam karne ke liye yah sabase acha samay hota he
 The comments workshop main kaam karne vaale anwar ke bhattije ne bataaya ki hamaari kaarigari hi hamaare liye sabakuch he
 This art of ours has been going on from generation to generation
 logon kaa ajrakh ke prati pyaar hi hamaare liye sabase bada tohfa he
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) bhuj main 2001 main aae bheeshan bukamp ke baad dhamadaka gaanv se ajrakhpur main aakar based sufian ismail khatari ke mutabik, yah gaanv bahut purana nahin he, lekin unka yah shilp 400 varshon se adhik purana he
 Sufiyan Ajrakh is from the 9th generation of printers
 unhone apane purvajon kii us kala ko aaj tak sanjo kar rakhaa he, jise unke purvaj sindh se lekar yahaan aae the
 Teaching design to a craftsman, Sufiyan said, “traditional Azrakh printing is a 16-step process through natural colors
 isamen 14 se 21 dinon kaa samay lagata he
 It also depends on how many colors will be in it and how many levels of block print will be used
 " The clothes are soaked overnight in water before dyeing them, so that excess starch comes out of them
 iske baad unhen dhoop main sukhaya jaataa he
 After drying they are dyed with Mayobralam color, after which they are again placed in the sun to dry
 is prakriya ke puraa hone ke baad shilpkaar paaramparik diginon vaale lakdi ke block ko chunate hai or phir unhen gond kii sahaayta se saavdhaneepurvak kapadon par chipkaaya jaataa he
 In Azrakh printing, after placing a block on the cloth, it has to be pressed
 isi prakaar shilpkaar blox ko chunate hai, unhen rangate hai or saavdhaneepurvak unhen kapadon par rakhkar dabaaya jaataa he
 After this process is completed, the clothes are washed and dried in the sun
 kapadon me istemaal hone vaali sabhi rang prakritik tareeke se banaae jate hai
 Ajrakh is called indigo in Arabic, which means the indigo plant
 yah paudha 1956 main kuccha main aae bukamp se pehle tak ilaake main har taraf dikhataa tha
 But, if some craftsmen are to be believed, the word Azrakh comes from 'aaj Rakh'
 ajrakhpur workshop ke aasapaas baari maatra main aapako lohe kaa chura dekhne ko milegaa
 Black color is made by mixing jaggery and gram flour in iron shred
 gaanv ke ek anya shilpkaar ismail anwar ne bataaya ki is rang ko banane main kam se kam 15 dinon kaa samay lagata he
 Red color is made from tamarind seeds and alum
 haldi se pilaa rang banaaya jaataa he or chooney kaa istemaal safed rang banane ke liye kiya jaataa he
 Anwar said, "traditionally, Azrakh printing was done only with natural colors, but now artificial colors are also used due to the demand for cheaper varieties
 kritrim rangon se kii gai pintring main kam samay lagata he
 " unhone bataaya ki kritrim pintring se ek sari ke taiyaar hone main do din kaa samay lagata he
 Whenever there is a high demand for goods, this is used
 kritrim rangon se taiyaar kiye gaye kapade kii keemat 50 se 60 rupye prati meter hoti he, par yadi kapade main anokhe dizin kaa print kiya gaya he, to uski keemat 100 rupye prati meter tak ja sakati he
 The story of Ajrakh was not always so colorful
 in shilpakaaron ke jivan main bhi ek bura samay aayaa tha, jab sabhi shilpakaaron ko apana sab kuch chhodkar duusari jagah janaa padaa or jivan jeene ke liye phir se sabhi sansadhano ko jhonkkar sabakuch dobaaraa shuru karnaa padaa
 Sufiyan said, 'today our craft is in great demand in the market
 tarun tahaliani jaise diziner ne mere saath kaam kiya he
 At the invitation of the designers, i got opportunities to go to different places and show my art
 aaj duniya ke bade-bade diziner hamaari kala ke bare main jaananaa chaahate hai
 " anwar ne bataaya ki diziner institute se bahut se bachche unki kala ko seekhney ke liye aate hai
 Artisans from all over the world come to see his exhibition
 unhone kaha ki unka yah kaam kisi bhi mausam main rukta nahin he, chaahe sardi ho yaa garmi
 His work continues in the hot summer of April as it is the best time to work
 tippaniyan Anwar's nephew, who works in the workshop, said that our workmanship is everything to us
 hamaari yah kala peedi dar peedi se chali aa rahi he
 People's love for Ajrakh is the biggest gift for us

 ) After the completion of this process, craftsmen choose wooden blocks with traditional designs and then glue them carefully onto the cloth with the help of glue
 ajrakh printig main kapade par block rakhane ke baad use dabaakar rakhana hota he
 Similarly, craftsmen choose blocks, color them and carefully place them on clothes and press them
 yah prakriya puri hone ke baad kapadon ko dhokar dhoop main sukhaya jaataa he
 All the colors used in clothes are made in a natural way
 ajrakh ko arabi bhashaa main indigo kaha jaataa he, jiskaa arth nil kaa paudha hota he
 This plant was visible everywhere in the area before the 1956 earthquake in Kutch
 lekin, kuch shilpakaaron kii maane to ajrakh shabd 'aaj rakh' se aayaa he

 lohe ke chure main gud or besan milakar kaala rang banaaya jaataa he
 Another craftsman from the village, Ismail Anwar, said that it takes at least 15 days to make this color
 imali ke beej or fitkaree se laal rang banaaya jaataa he

 " He said that it takes two days to prepare a saree with artificial pintering
 jab kabhi maal kii zyada maang hoti he, to isi kaa istemaal kiya jaataa he
 a fabric made of artificial colors costs 50 to 60 rupees per meter, but if the fabric is printed with a unique design, then the price can go up to 100 rupees per meter

 ) kapadon me istemaal hone vaali sabhi rang prakritik tareeke se banaae jate hai
 Ajrakh is called indigo in Arabic, which means the indigo plant
 yah paudha 1956 main kuccha main aae bukamp se pehle tak ilaake main har taraf dikhataa tha
 But, if some craftsmen are to be believed, the word Azrakh comes from 'aaj Rakh'
 ajrakhpur workshop ke aasapaas baari maatra main aapako lohe kaa chura dekhne ko milegaa
 Black color is made by mixing jaggery and gram flour in iron shred
 gaanv ke ek anya shilpkaar ismail anwar ne bataaya ki is rang ko banane main kam se kam 15 dinon kaa samay lagata he
 Red color is made from tamarind seeds and alum
 haldi se pilaa rang banaaya jaataa he or chooney kaa istemaal safed rang banane ke liye kiya jaataa he
 Anwar said, "traditionally, Azrakh printing was done only with natural colors, but now artificial colors are also used due to the demand for cheaper varieties
 kritrim rangon se kii gai pintring main kam samay lagata he
 " unhone bataaya ki kritrim pintring se ek sari ke taiyaar hone main do din kaa samay lagata he
 Whenever there is a high demand for goods, this is used
 kritrim rangon se taiyaar kiye gaye kapade kii keemat 50 se 60 rupye prati meter hoti he, par yadi kapade main anokhe dizin kaa print kiya gaya he, to uski keemat 100 rupye prati meter tak ja sakati he
 The story of Ajrakh was not always so colorful
 in shilpakaaron ke jivan main bhi ek bura samay aayaa tha, jab sabhi shilpakaaron ko apana sab kuch chhodkar duusari jagah janaa padaa or jivan jeene ke liye phir se sabhi sansadhano ko jhonkkar sabakuch dobaaraa shuru karnaa padaa
 Sufiyan said, 'today our craft is in great demand in the market
 tarun tahaliani jaise diziner ne mere saath kaam kiya he

 aaj duniya ke bade-bade diziner hamaari kala ke bare main jaananaa chaahate hai
 " anwar ne bataaya ki diziner institute se bahut se bachche unki kala ko seekhney ke liye aate hai
 Artisans from all over the world come to see his exhibition
 unhone kaha ki unka yah kaam kisi bhi mausam main rukta nahin he, chaahe sardi ho yaa garmi
 His work continues in the hot summer of April as it is the best time to work
 tippaniyan Anwar's nephew, who works in the workshop, said that our workmanship is everything to us
 hamaari yah kala peedi dar peedi se chali aa rahi he

 dilli airport (delhi Airport) par imigration vibhaag (immigration Department) ke saamne aisa maamla saamne aayaa jisase wo hairaan rah gaye
 a person was traveling after hiding his age
 68 saal kaa ek vyakti 89 saal kaa bataakar videsh yatra karne ke liye ja rahaa tha
 The Immigration Department looked like a young man and was caught
 uske passport main naam karnel singh or janmatithi 20 oktober 1930 thi
 Investigation revealed that his real name is Gurdeep Singh, who hails from Moga Punjab and his real date of birth is 16 March 1951
 (89 saal kaa banakar yatra kar rahaa tha 68 varshiya shaks
 ) After which the immigration department handed over the man to the police
 police ke mutabik wo pehali baar 1995 main apane passport par honkong gaya

 wo honkong kii nagarikta lenaa chahta tha
 But even after much effort, he could not get a permanent Hong Kong ID

 In such a situation, he got a fake passport made
 iske baad usne 2006 main ek agent ko contact kiya
 He got his fake passport made by the name of Karnail Singh
 farji passport ke mutabik 68 varshiya gurdeep singh kii umr 89 saal ho gai
 Since then he has been traveling in the same passport since 2008, so he obtained a permanent identity card in Hong Kong
 11 saal se do deshon ko dhul jhunk rahaa tha
 Team India, which created history in this country for the first time in 72 years after defeating the host Kangaroos in the Test series, will now look to win a bilateral (bilateral) ODI series for the first time on Australian soil
 team india ne australia kii dharti par 12 vanade siries kheli hai magar isamen ek siries ko chhod diya jaae to baaki sabhi multination vanade siries raheen
 The only bilateral ODI series between India and Australia was played in the year 2016
 paanch maichon kii is siries main bharat ko 1-4 se haar jhelni padi thi
 Looking at the overall record, India has played a total of 48 odis in Australia, in which they won 11, lost 35 matches and 2 remained unbeaten
 aise main test main kamaal karne vaali team india ab pehali baar australia main mejabaan kangaaroon ke khilaaf koi bilatural (dwipaksheeya) vanade siries jeetna chaahegi
 indiateam India has won two ODI series in Australia, but it was not a bilateral (bilateral) but multinational ODI series
 bharat ne 1984-1985 main benson and hejes world championships toornament jeeta tha
 After this, India named the Commonwealth Bank ODI tri-series in 2007-2008
 1984-1985 main bharat ne sunil gavaskar kii captaini main kangaaroon kii dharti par multination vanade toornament jeeta tha
 In one match of this tournament, India had beaten Australia by a memorable win by eight wickets
 emsiji par 1984-1985 main benson and hejes world championships bharat or australia donon ke liye hi bahut mahatvapurn thi
 To knockout Team India, Australia needed to stop the visiting team on a score of 160 runs after scoring 223 runs
 lekin, roger binni (27 / 3) kii shandaar gendbaaji kii badaulat bharat ne pehle ballebaaji karne utari australia ko 163 ran par olout kar diya
 After that Krishnamachari Srikkanth beat the Australian bowlers fiercely and gave the Indian team a memorable eight-wicket victory
 shrikant ne apni 93 ran kii naabad pari main 12 chauke jamaaye
 India then went on to beat Pakistan by eight wickets to win the Benson & Hedges World Championship trophy
 2007-2008 main maahi kii captaini kaa chalaa tha jaadu2007-2008 kaamanwealth bank siries main mahendra singh dhoni kii captaini vaali team india ne shandaar pradarshan kiya tha
 In this tournament, Gautam Gambhir scored 440 runs while Sachin Tendulkar scored 399 runs
 bharat ke liye eshanth sharma ne 14 irfan pathan ne 11 or praveen kumaar ne 10 wicket hasil kiye
 In the first and second finals of this tri-series, Sachin Tendulkar scored 117 and 91 runs respectively
 tab sachin ne australian dharti par apana pehla vanade shatak jamaaya tha
 India won the trophy after winning the second final
